defined_text = {
	name = getBunkerQuality
	text = {
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { HGR_Bunker_Quality > 74 }
		}
		localization_key = HGR_Quality_4
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { HGR_Bunker_Quality > 49 }
		}
		localization_key = HGR_Quality_3
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { HGR_Bunker_Quality > 24 }
		}
		localization_key = HGR_Quality_2
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			always = yes
		}
		localization_key = HGR_Quality_1
	}
}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			SSW = {
				check_variable = { HGR_Influence_Balance < 41 }
			}
		}
		localization_key = GFX_HGR_Missile_Burg
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			SSW = {
				check_variable = { HGR_Influence_Balance > 59 }
			}
		}
		localization_key = GFX_HGR_Missile_Ger
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			SSW = {
				AND = {
					check_variable = { HGR_Influence_Balance < 60 }
					check_variable = { HGR_Influence_Balance > 40 }
				}
			}
		}
		localization_key = GFX_HGR_Missile_Neu
	}
}

defined_text = {
	name = HGRgetAlsaceLorraine_Grid
	text = {
		trigger = {
			42 = {
				controller = {
					AND = {
						NOT = {
							tag = LHH
						}
						controls_state = 28
						controls_state = 51
						controls_state = 8
						check_variable = { HGR_Influence_Balance < 41 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		localization_key = GFX_HGR_AlsaceLorraine_Grid_Burg
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			42 = {
				controller = {
					AND = {
						NOT = {
							tag = LHH
						}
						controls_state = 28
						controls_state = 51
						controls_state = 8

						check_variable = { HGR_Influence_Balance > 59 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		localization_key = GFX_HGR_AlsaceLorraine_Grid_Ger
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			42 = {
				controller = {
					AND = {
						NOT = {
							tag = LHH
						}
						controls_state = 28
						controls_state = 51
						controls_state = 8
						AND = {
							check_variable = { HGR_Influence_Balance < 60 }
							check_variable = { HGR_Influence_Balance > 40 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		localization_key = GFX_HGR_AlsaceLorraine_Grid_Neu
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			tag = GER
		}
		localization_key = GFX_HGR_AlsaceLorraine_Grid_Empty
	}
}

defined_text = {
	name = HGRgetLHHLOVE
	text = {
		trigger = {
			LHH = {
				is_in_faction_with = GER
			}
		}
		localization_key = HGR_GUI_TEXT_95to100
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			LHH = {
				is_in_faction_with = BRG
			}
		}
		localization_key = HGR_GUI_TEXT_0to5
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			LHH = {
				check_variable = { HGR_Influence_Balance > 59 }
			}
		}
		localization_key = HGR_GUI_TEXT_60to95
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			LHH = {
				AND = {
					check_variable = { HGR_Influence_Balance < 60 }
					check_variable = { HGR_Influence_Balance > 40 }
				}
			}
		}
		localization_key = HGR_GUI_TEXT_40to60
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			LHH = {
				check_variable = { HGR_Influence_Balance < 41 }
			}
		}
		localization_key = HGR_GUI_TEXT_5to40
	}
}
